            <div class="article-inner-container" style="max-width:1280px;">
             <div class="inset-container Mx-a">
              <div class="GridTable">
               <div class="D-tbr row-template">
                <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-left">

                   <div class="D-tbr row-content">
                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-left Pend-20" style="width:305px;max-width:305px;">
                     <h1 class="Font-A-6-110 title W-100" id="article-aft-title-117296117162">
                      First Look: Jared Leto as the Joker in 'Suicide Squad'
                     </h1>
                     <div class="attribution-component D-b W-100" id="article-aft-attribution-117296117162" style="max-width:305px;">
                      <div class="author-info author-info-text-first Pt-10 W-100 Bd-t Bd-b Bdstart-0 Bdend-0">
                       <div class="GridTable W-100">
                        <div class="D-tbr">
                         <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t">
                          <cite class="byline col D-b Fs-n" style="padding-bottom:15px;">
                           <span class="author-name Font-C-2-140 D-b">
                            <a class="attribution-name Font-C-2-140 Fw-b Whs-n" data-ylk="t1:a2;t2:article;t3:cat;t8:4d01e2b6-7660-394a-91f7-0395b353391b;t9:17;elm:itm;elmt:link;itc:0" href="http://variety.com/" style="color:#000;" target="_blank">
                             Variety
                            </a>
                           </span>
                           <time class="date Font-C-2-140 Fw-n D-b">
                            <span>
                             April 25, 2015
                            </span>
                           </time>
                          </cite>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-right" style="max-width:500px;">
                     <div class="text-body-wrapper W-100 Font-B-1-160">
                      <noscript>
                      </noscript>
                      <div class="text-body W-100 Font-B-1-160" id="article-aft-text-body-117296117162" style="color:#222222;max-width:500px;">
                       <div class="body read-more-cut">
                        <div class="pre-cut" style="height:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;">
                         <figure>
                          <img alt="First Look: Jared Leto as the Joker in 'Suicide Squad'" height="594" src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w460/6fdef8f72d6cb5e7a6be17ea59a983c66c58cf6d.png" width="460"/>
                         </figure>
                         <p>
                          By
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:4d01e2b6-7660-394a-91f7-0395b353391b;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://variety.com/author/justin-kroll/" target="_blank">
                           Justin Kroll
                          </a>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          After teasing
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:4d01e2b6-7660-394a-91f7-0395b353391b;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://variety.com/t/jared-leto/" target="_blank">
                           Jared Leto
                          </a>
                          s look in Warner Bros. upcoming DC movie
                          <i>
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:4d01e2b6-7660-394a-91f7-0395b353391b;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://variety.com/t/suicide-squad/" target="_blank">
                            Suicide Squad
                           </a>
                          </i>
                          for the last two weeks, director David Ayer has now released the first official
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:4d01e2b6-7660-394a-91f7-0395b353391b;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://variety411.com/us/los-angeles/stock-footage-photos/" target="_blank" title="photo">
                           photo
                          </a>
                          of the Oscar-winner in full
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:4d01e2b6-7660-394a-91f7-0395b353391b;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://variety.com/t/joker/" target="_blank">
                           Joker
                          </a>
                          makeup.
                         </p>
                         <figure>
                          <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-cards="hidden" lang="en">
                           <p>
                            The Suicide Squad wishes you a Happy Anniversary Mr. J!
                            <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:4d01e2b6-7660-394a-91f7-0395b353391b;t9:18;itc:0" href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/Joker75?src=hash" target="_blank">
                             #Joker75
                            </a>
                            <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:4d01e2b6-7660-394a-91f7-0395b353391b;t9:18;itc:0" href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/SuicideSquad?src=hash" target="_blank">
                             #SuicideSquad
                            </a>
                            <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:4d01e2b6-7660-394a-91f7-0395b353391b;t9:18;itc:0" href="https://twitter.com/WarnerBrosEnt" target="_blank">
                             @WarnerBrosEnt
                            </a>
                            <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:4d01e2b6-7660-394a-91f7-0395b353391b;t9:18;itc:0" href="https://twitter.com/DCComics" target="_blank">
                             @DCComics
                            </a>
                            <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:4d01e2b6-7660-394a-91f7-0395b353391b;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://t.co/LZXz0x947Q" target="_blank">
                             pic.twitter.com/LZXz0x947Q
                            </a>
                           </p>
                            David Ayer (@DavidAyerMovies)
                           <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:4d01e2b6-7660-394a-91f7-0395b353391b;t9:18;itc:0" href="https://twitter.com/DavidAyerMovies/status/591761248859123713" target="_blank">
                            April 25, 2015
                           </a>
                          </blockquote>
                         </figure>
                         <p>
                          The photo promises another dark and wild version of the popular comic-book villain.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <i>
                           Suicide Squad
                          </i>
                          , co-starring Will Smith and Margot Robbie, is currently shooting in Toronto. The story centers on a group of supervillains hired for a suicide mission by the government that if accomplished would give them a clean slate. The problem: The mission is considered a suicide mission.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          It opens nationwide August 5, 2016.
                         </p>
